<pr_description>
SpinnerView AutoSpin does not advance animation
## Describe the bug

I noticed a spinner in my app was no longer functioning. I ran the SpinnerStyles scenario and it is not working there either.

## To Reproduce

1. Run the following code:
```csharp
namespace UICatalog.Scenarios;

[ScenarioMetadata ("Spinner Demo", "Minimal SpinnerView demo with auto-spin.")]
[ScenarioCategory ("Controls")]
[ScenarioCategory ("Progress")]
public class SpinnerDemo : Scenario
{
    public override void Main ()
    {
        using IApplication app = Application.Create ();
        app.Init ();

        using Window main = new () { Title = GetQuitKeyAndName () };

        SpinnerView spinner = new ()
        {
            X = Pos.Center (),
            Y = Pos.Center (),
            AutoSpin = true
        };

        main.Add (spinner);

        app.Run (main);
    }
}
```

2. Expected behavior: There should be a spinner, spinning.
3. Actual behavior: The first character of the spinner sequence is displayed, without changing.

## Note:
Manually advancing the spinner with AdvanceAnimation() does work.

## Environment

Tested on Windows 11 with dotnet, windows, and ansi drivers.

### Terminal.Gui Version

v2.0.0-beta.1-113-g6c4f01d6d

    11	/// <summary>Displays a spinning glyph or combinations of glyphs to indicate progress or activity</summary>
    12	/// <remarks>
    13	///     By default, animation only occurs when you call <see cref="SpinnerView.AdvanceAnimation(bool)"/>. Use
    14	///     <see cref="AutoSpin"/> to make the automate calls to <see cref="SpinnerView.AdvanceAnimation(bool)"/>.
    15	/// </remarks>
    16	public class SpinnerView : View, IDesignable
    17	{
    18	    private const int DEFAULT_DELAY = 130;
    19	    private static readonly SpinnerStyle DEFAULT_STYLE = new SpinnerStyle.Line ();
    20	
    21	    private bool _bounce = DEFAULT_STYLE.SpinBounce;
    22	    private bool _bounceReverse;
    23	    private int _currentIdx;
    24	    private int _delay = DEFAULT_STYLE.SpinDelay;
    25	    private DateTime _lastRender = DateTime.MinValue;
    26	    private string [] _sequence = DEFAULT_STYLE.Sequence;
    27	    private SpinnerStyle _style = DEFAULT_STYLE;
    28	    private object? _timeout;
    29	
    30	    /// <summary>Creates a new instance of the <see cref="SpinnerView"/> class.</summary>
    31	    public SpinnerView ()
    32	    {
    33	        Width = Dim.Auto (minimumContentDim: 1);
    34	        Height = Dim.Auto (minimumContentDim: 1);
    35	        _delay = DEFAULT_DELAY;
    36	        _bounce = false;
    37	        SpinReverse = false;
    38	        SetStyle (DEFAULT_STYLE);
    39	
    40	        AdvanceAnimation ();
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    /// <summary>
    44	    ///     Gets or sets whether spinning should occur automatically or be manually triggered (e.g. from a background
    45	    ///     task).
    46	    /// </summary>
    47	    public bool AutoSpin
    48	    {
    49	        get => _timeout != null;
    50	        set
    51	        {
    52	            if (value)
    53	            {
    54	                AddAutoSpinTimeout ();
    55	            }
    56	            else
    57	            {
    58	                RemoveAutoSpinTimeout ();
    59	            }
    60	        }
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    /// <summary>
    64	    ///     Gets whether the current spinner style contains emoji or other special characters. Does not check Custom
    65	    ///     sequences.
    66	    /// </summary>
    67	    public bool HasSpecialCharacters => _style.HasSpecialCharacters;
    68	
    69	    /// <summary>Gets whether the current spinner style contains only ASCII characters.  Also checks Custom sequences.</summary>
    70	    public bool IsAsciiOnly => GetIsAsciiOnly ();
    71	
    72	    /// <summary>Gets or sets the animation frames used to animate the spinner.</summary>
    73	    public string [] Sequence
    74	    {
    75	        get => _sequence;
    76	        set => SetSequence (value);
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    /// <summary>
    80	    ///     Gets or sets whether spinner should go back and forth through the frames rather than going to the end and
    81	    ///     starting again at the beginning.
    82	    /// </summary>
    83	    public bool SpinBounce
    84	    {
    85	        get => _bounce;
    86	        set => SetBounce (value);
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    /// <summary>Gets or sets the number of milliseconds to wait between characters in the animation.</summary>
    90	    /// <remarks>
    91	    ///     This is the maximum speed the spinner will rotate at.  You still need to call
    92	    ///     <see cref="SpinnerView.AdvanceAnimation(bool)"/> or <see cref="SpinnerView.AutoSpin"/> to advance/start animation.
    93	    /// </remarks>
    94	    public int SpinDelay
    95	    {
    96	        get => _delay;
    97	        set => SetDelay (value);
    98	    }
    99	
   100	    /// <summary>
   101	    ///     Gets or sets whether spinner should go through the frames in reverse order. If SpinBounce is true, this sets
   102	    ///     the starting order.
   103	    /// </summary>
   104	    public bool SpinReverse { get; set; }
   105	
   106	    /// <summary>Gets or sets the Style used to animate the spinner.</summary>
   107	    public SpinnerStyle Style
   108	    {
   109	        get => _style;
   110	        set => SetStyle (value);
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    /// <summary>
   114	    ///     Advances the animation frame and notifies main loop that repainting needs to happen. Repeated calls are
   115	    ///     ignored based on <see cref="SpinDelay"/>.
   116	    /// </summary>
   117	    /// <remarks>Ensure this method is called on the main UI thread e.g. via <see cref="IApplication.Invoke(Action)"/></remarks>
   118	    public void AdvanceAnimation (bool setNeedsDraw = true)
   119	    {
   120	        if (DateTime.Now - _lastRender > TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds (SpinDelay))
   121	        {
   122	            if (Sequence is { Length: > 1 })
   123	            {
   124	                var d = 1;
   125	
   126	                if ((_bounceReverse && !SpinReverse) || (!_bounceReverse && SpinReverse))
   127	                {
   128	                    d = -1;
   129	                }
   130	
   131	                _currentIdx += d;
   132	
   133	                if (_currentIdx >= Sequence.Length)
   134	                {
   135	                    if (SpinBounce)
   136	                    {
   137	                        _bounceReverse = !SpinReverse;
   138	
   139	                        _currentIdx = Sequence.Length - 1;
   140	                    }
   141	                    else
   142	                    {
   143	                        _currentIdx = 0;
   144	                    }
   145	                }
   146	
   147	                if (_currentIdx < 0)
   148	                {
   149	                    if (SpinBounce)
   150	                    {
   151	                        _bounceReverse = SpinReverse;
   152	
   153	                        _currentIdx = 1;
   154	                    }
   155	                    else
   156	                    {
   157	                        _currentIdx = Sequence.Length - 1;
   158	                    }
   159	                }
   160	            }
   161	
   162	            _lastRender = DateTime.Now;
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        if (setNeedsDraw)
   166	        {
   167	            SetNeedsDraw ();
   168	        }
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   172	    protected override bool OnClearingViewport () { return true; }
   173	
   174	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   175	    protected override bool OnDrawingContent (DrawContext? context)
   176	    {
   177	        Render ();
   178	
   179	        return true;
   180	    }
   181	
   182	    /// <summary>
   183	    ///     Renders the current frame of the spinner.
   184	    /// </summary>
   185	    public void Render ()
   186	    {
   187	        if (Sequence is { Length: > 0 } && _currentIdx < Sequence.Length)
   188	        {
   189	            Move (Viewport.X, Viewport.Y);
   190	            AddStr (Sequence [_currentIdx]);
   191	        }
   192	    }
   193	
   194	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   195	    protected override void Dispose (bool disposing)
   196	    {
   197	        RemoveAutoSpinTimeout ();
   198	
   199	        base.Dispose (disposing);
   200	    }
   201	
   202	    private void AddAutoSpinTimeout ()
   203	    {
   204	        // Only add timeout if we are initialized and not already spinning
   205	        if (App is { } && (_timeout is { } || !App.Initialized))
   206	        {
   207	            return;
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        _timeout = App?.AddTimeout (
   211	                                           TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds (SpinDelay),
   212	                                           () =>
   213	                                           {
   214	                                               App.Invoke ((_) => AdvanceAnimation ());
   215	
   216	                                               return true;
   217	                                           }
   218	                                          );
   219	    }
   220	
   221	    private bool GetIsAsciiOnly ()
   222	    {
   223	        if (HasSpecialCharacters)
   224	        {
   225	            return false;
   226	        }
   227	
   228	        if (_sequence is { Length: > 0 })
   229	        {
   230	            foreach (string frame in _sequence)
   231	            {
   232	                foreach (char c in frame)
   233	                {
   234	                    if (!char.IsAscii (c))
   235	                    {
   236	                        return false;
   237	                    }
   238	                }
   239	            }
   240	
   241	            return true;
   242	        }
   243	
   244	        return true;
   245	    }
   246	
   247	    private int GetSpinnerWidth ()
   248	    {
   249	        var max = 0;
   250	
   251	        if (_sequence is { Length: > 0 })
   252	        {
   253	            foreach (string frame in _sequence)
   254	            {
   255	                if (frame.Length > max)
   256	                {
   257	                    max = frame.Length;
   258	                }
   259	            }
   260	        }
   261	
   262	        return max;
   263	    }
   264	
   265	    private void RemoveAutoSpinTimeout ()
   266	    {
   267	        if (_timeout is { })
   268	        {
   269	            App?.RemoveTimeout (_timeout);
   270	            _timeout = null;
   271	        }
   272	    }
   273	
   274	    private void SetBounce (bool bounce) { _bounce = bounce; }
   275	
   276	    private void SetDelay (int delay)
   277	    {
   278	        if (delay > -1)
   279	        {
   280	            _delay = delay;
   281	        }
   282	    }
   283	
   284	    private void SetSequence (string [] frames)
   285	    {
   286	        if (frames is { Length: > 0 })
   287	        {
   288	            _style = new SpinnerStyle.Custom ();
   289	            _sequence = frames;
   290	            Width = GetSpinnerWidth ();
   291	        }
   292	    }
   293	
   294	    private void SetStyle (SpinnerStyle? style)
   295	    {
   296	        if (style is { })
   297	        {
   298	            _style = style;
   299	            _sequence = style.Sequence;
   300	            _delay = style.SpinDelay;
   301	            _bounce = style.SpinBounce;
   302	            Width = GetSpinnerWidth ();
   303	        }
   304	    }
   305	
   306	    bool IDesignable.EnableForDesign ()
   307	    {
   308	        Style = new SpinnerStyle.Points ();
   309	        SpinReverse = true;
   310	        AutoSpin = true;
   311	
   312	        return true;
   313	    }
   314	}

     1	using System.Diagnostics;
     2	using System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;

     7	internal partial class ApplicationImpl
     8	{
     9	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    10	    public int? MainThreadId { get; set; }
    11	
    12	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    13	    public bool Initialized { get; set; }
    14	
    15	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    16	    public event EventHandler<EventArgs<bool>>? InitializedChanged;
    17	
    18	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    19	    [RequiresUnreferencedCode ("AOT")]
    20	    [RequiresDynamicCode ("AOT")]
    21	    public IApplication Init (string? driverName = null)
    22	    {
    23	        if (Initialized)
    24	        {
    25	            Logging.Error ("Init called multiple times without shutdown, aborting.");
    26	
    27	            throw new InvalidOperationException ("Init called multiple times without Shutdown");
    28	        }
    29	
    30	        MainThreadId = Thread.CurrentThread.ManagedThreadId;
    31	
    32	        Trace.Lifecycle (MainThreadId?.ToString (), "Init", $"driverName: {driverName}");
    33	
    34	        // Thread-safe fence check: Ensure we're not mixing application models
    35	        // Use lock to make check-and-set atomic
    36	        lock (_modelUsageLock)
    37	        {
    38	            // If this is a legacy static instance and instance-based model was used, throw
    39	            if (this == _instance && ModelUsage == ApplicationModelUsage.InstanceBased)
    40	            {
    41	                throw new InvalidOperationException (ERROR_LEGACY_AFTER_MODERN);
    42	            }
    43	
    44	            // If this is an instance-based instance and legacy static model was used, throw
    45	            if (this != _instance && ModelUsage == ApplicationModelUsage.LegacyStatic)
    46	            {
    47	                throw new InvalidOperationException (ERROR_MODERN_AFTER_LEGACY);
    48	            }
    49	
    50	            // If no model has been set yet, set it now based on which instance this is
    51	            if (ModelUsage == ApplicationModelUsage.None)
    52	            {
    53	                ModelUsage = this == _instance ? ApplicationModelUsage.LegacyStatic : ApplicationModelUsage.InstanceBased;
    54	            }
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace (driverName))
    58	        {
    59	            _driverName = driverName;
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace (_driverName))
    63	        {
    64	            _driverName = ForceDriver;
    65	        }
    66	
    67	        // Reset keyboard to ensure fresh state with default bindings
    68	        _keyboard = new ApplicationKeyboard { App = this };
    69	
    70	        CreateDriver (_driverName);
    71	
    72	        Initialized = true;
    73	
    74	        RaiseInitializedChanged (this, new EventArgs<bool> (true));
    75	        SubscribeDriverEvents ();
    76	
    77	        SynchronizationContext.SetSynchronizationContext (new SynchronizationContext ());
    78	
    79	        _result = null;
    80	
    81	        // Raise static event for modern instance-based model
    82	        Application.RaiseInstanceInitialized (this);
    83	
    84	        return this;
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    #region IDisposable Implementation
    88	
    89	    private bool _disposed;
    90	
    91	    /// <summary>
    92	    ///     Disposes the application instance and releases all resources.
    93	    /// </summary>
    94	    /// <remarks>
    95	    ///     <para>
    96	    ///         This method implements the <see cref="IDisposable"/> pattern and performs the same cleanup
    97	    ///         as <see cref="IDisposable.Dispose"/>, but without returning a result.
    98	    ///     </para>
    99	    ///     <para>
   100	    ///         After calling <see cref="Dispose()"/>, use <see cref="GetResult"/> or <see cref="IApplication.GetResult{T}"/>
   101	    ///         to retrieve the result from the last run session.
   102	    ///     </para>
   103	    /// </remarks>
   104	    public void Dispose ()
   105	    {
   106	        Dispose (true);
   107	        GC.SuppressFinalize (this);
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    /// <summary>
   111	    ///     Disposes the application instance and releases all resources.
   112	    /// </summary>
   113	    /// <param name="disposing">
   114	    ///     <see langword="true"/> if called from <see cref="Dispose()"/>;
   115	    ///     <see langword="false"/> if called from finalizer.
   116	    /// </param>
   117	    protected virtual void Dispose (bool disposing)
   118	    {
   119	        if (_disposed)
   120	        {
   121	            return;
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        if (disposing)
   125	        {
   126	            // Dispose managed resources
   127	            DisposeCore ();
   128	        }
   129	
   130	        // For the singleton instance (legacy Application.Init/Shutdown pattern),
   131	        // we need to allow re-initialization after disposal. This enables:
   132	        // Application.Init() -> Application.Shutdown() -> Application.Init()
   133	        // For modern instance-based usage, this doesn't matter as new instances are created.
   134	        if (this == _instance)
   135	        {
   136	            // Reset disposed flag to allow re-initialization
   137	            _disposed = false;
   138	        }
   139	        else
   140	        {
   141	            // For instance-based usage, mark as disposed
   142	            _disposed = true;
   143	        }
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    /// <summary>
   147	    ///     Core disposal logic - same as Shutdown() but without returning result.
   148	    /// </summary>
   149	    private void DisposeCore ()
   150	    {
   151	        // Stop the coordinator if running
   152	        Coordinator?.Stop ();
   153	
   154	        // Capture state before cleanup
   155	        bool wasInitialized = Initialized;
   156	
   157	        // Raise static event for modern instance-based model BEFORE assertions
   158	        // This allows test code to unsubscribe from instance events before we check
   159	        Application.RaiseInstanceDisposed (this);
   160	
   161	#if DEBUG
   162	
   163	        // Check that all Application events have no remaining subscribers BEFORE clearing them
   164	        // Only check if we were actually initialized
   165	        if (wasInitialized)
   166	        {
   167	            AssertNoEventSubscribers (nameof (Iteration), Iteration);
   168	            AssertNoEventSubscribers (nameof (SessionBegun), SessionBegun);
   169	            AssertNoEventSubscribers (nameof (SessionEnded), SessionEnded);
   170	            AssertNoEventSubscribers (nameof (ScreenChanged), ScreenChanged);
   171	
   172	            //AssertNoEventSubscribers (nameof (InitializedChanged), InitializedChanged);
   173	        }
   174	#endif
   175	
   176	        // Clean up all application state (including sync context)
   177	        // ResetState handles the case where Initialized is false
   178	        ResetState ();
   179	
   180	        // Configuration manager diagnostics
   181	        ConfigurationManager.PrintJsonErrors ();
   182	
   183	        // Raise the initialized changed event to notify shutdown
   184	        if (wasInitialized)
   185	        {
   186	            bool init = Initialized; // Will be false after ResetState
   187	            RaiseInitializedChanged (this, new EventArgs<bool> (in init));
   188	        }
   189	
   190	        // Clear the event to prevent memory leaks
   191	        InitializedChanged = null;
   192	    }
   193	
   194	    #endregion IDisposable Implementation
   195	
   196	    /// <summary>Shutdown an application initialized with <see cref="Init"/>.</summary>
   197	    [Obsolete ("Use Dispose() or a using statement instead. This method will be removed in a future version.")]
   198	    public object? Shutdown ()
   199	    {
   200	        // Shutdown is now just a wrapper around Dispose that returns the result
   201	        object? result = GetResult ();
   202	        Dispose ();
   203	
   204	        return result;
   205	    }
   206	
   207	    private object? _result;
   208	
   209	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   210	    public object? GetResult () => _result;
   211	
   212	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   213	    public void ResetState (bool ignoreDisposed = false)
   214	    {
   215	        // Shutdown is the bookend for Init. As such it needs to clean up all resources
   216	        // Init created. Apps that do any threading will need to code defensively for this.
   217	        // e.g. see Issue #537
   218	
   219	        Trace.Lifecycle (MainThreadId?.ToString (), "Shutdown");
   220	
   221	        // === 0. Stop all timers ===
   222	        TimedEvents.StopAll ();
   223	
   224	        // === 1. Stop all running runnables ===
   225	        foreach (SessionToken token in SessionStack!.Reverse ())
   226	        {
   227	            if (token.Runnable is { })
   228	            {
   229	                End (token);
   230	            }
   231	        }
   232	
   233	        // === 2. Close and dispose popover ===
   234	        // Any popovers added to Popover have their lifetime controlled by Popover
   235	        Popovers?.Dispose ();
   236	        Popovers = null;
   237	
   238	        // === 3. Clean up runnables ===
   239	        SessionStack?.Clear ();
   240	
   241	#if DEBUG_IDISPOSABLE
   242	
   243	        // Don't dispose the TopRunnable. It's up to caller dispose it
   244	        if (View.EnableDebugIDisposableAsserts && !ignoreDisposed && TopRunnableView is { })
   245	        {
   246	            Debug.Assert (TopRunnableView.WasDisposed, TopRunnableView.ToDebugString ());
   247	        }
   248	#endif
   249	
   250	        // === 4. Clean up driver ===
   251	        // Capture-and-null to avoid race when Dispose is called concurrently from
   252	        // multiple threads (e.g. AppTestHelper background thread + test thread).
   253	        // Null Driver first so concurrent callers see null and skip cleanup.
   254	        IDriver? driver = Driver;
   255	        Driver = null;
   256	
   257	        if (driver is { })
   258	        {
   259	            // Unsubscribe using the captured local since Driver property is now null
   260	            driver.SizeChanged -= Driver_SizeChanged;
   261	            driver.KeyDown -= Driver_KeyDown;
   262	            driver.KeyUp -= Driver_KeyUp;
   263	            driver.MouseEvent -= Driver_MouseEvent;
   264	            driver.Dispose ();
   265	        }
   266	
   267	        // === 5. Clear run state ===
   268	        Iteration = null;
   269	        SessionBegun = null;
   270	        SessionEnded = null;
   271	        StopAfterFirstIteration = false;
   272	        ClearScreenNextIteration = false;
   273	
   274	        // === 6. Reset input systems ===
   275	        // Dispose keyboard and mouse to unsubscribe from events
   276	        // Mouse and Keyboard will be lazy-initialized on next access
   277	        if (_keyboard is IDisposable keyboardDisposable)
   278	        {
   279	            keyboardDisposable.Dispose ();
   280	        }
   281	        _keyboard = null;
   282	
   283	        if (_mouse is IDisposable mouseDisposable)
   284	        {
   285	            mouseDisposable.Dispose ();
   286	        }
   287	        _mouse = null;
   288	
   289	        // === 7. Clear navigation and screen state ===
   290	        ScreenChanged = null;
   291	
   292	        // === 8. Reset initialization state ===
   293	        Initialized = false;
   294	        MainThreadId = null;
   295	
   296	        // === 9. Reset synchronization context ===
   297	        // IMPORTANT: Always reset sync context, even if not initialized
   298	        // This ensures cleanup works correctly even if Shutdown is called without Init
   299	        // Reset synchronization context to allow the user to run async/await,
   300	        // as the main loop has been ended, the synchronization context from
   301	        // gui.cs does no longer process any callbacks. See #1084 for more details:
   302	        // (https://github.com/gui-cs/Terminal.Gui/issues/1084).
   303	        SynchronizationContext.SetSynchronizationContext (null);
   304	
   305	        // === 10. Unsubscribe from Application static property change events ===
   306	        UnsubscribeApplicationEvents ();
   307	    }
   308	
   309	    /// <summary>
   310	    ///     Raises the <see cref="InitializedChanged"/> event.
   311	    /// </summary>
   312	    internal void RaiseInitializedChanged (object sender, EventArgs<bool> e) => InitializedChanged?.Invoke (sender, e);
   313	
   314	#if DEBUG
   315	    /// <summary>
   316	    ///     DEBUG ONLY: Asserts that an event has no remaining subscribers.
   317	    /// </summary>
   318	    /// <param name="eventName">The name of the event for diagnostic purposes.</param>
   319	    /// <param name="eventDelegate">The event delegate to check.</param>
   320	    private static void AssertNoEventSubscribers (string eventName, Delegate? eventDelegate)
   321	    {
   322	        if (eventDelegate is null)
   323	        {
   324	            return;
   325	        }
   326	
   327	        Delegate [] subscribers = eventDelegate.GetInvocationList ();
   328	
   329	        if (subscribers.Length <= 0)
   330	        {
   331	            return;
   332	        }
   333	        string subscriberInfo = string.Join (", ", subscribers.Select (d => $"{d.Method.DeclaringType?.Name}.{d.Method.Name}"));
   334	
   335	        Debug.Fail ($"Application.{eventName} has {subscribers.Length} remaining subscriber(s) after Shutdown: {subscriberInfo}");
   336	    }
   337	#endif
   338	
   339	    private void OnForceDriverChanged (object? sender, ValueChangedEventArgs<string> e) => ForceDriver = e.NewValue;
   340	
   341	    /// <summary>
   342	    ///     Unsubscribes from Application static property change events.
   343	    /// </summary>
   344	    private void UnsubscribeApplicationEvents () => Application.ForceDriverChanged -= OnForceDriverChanged;
   345	}

2026-05-29 12:41:06,415 - INFO - swea-agent-gui-cs__Terminal.Gui-4882 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the flow better. Let me trace through the issue:

1. `SpinnerView` constructor calls `AdvanceAnimation()` at line 40, which sets `_lastRender = DateTime.Now`.
2. When `AutoSpin = true` is set, `AddAutoSpinTimeout()` is called.
3. In `AddAutoSpinTimeout()`:
   - Line 205: `if (App is { } && (_timeout is { } || !App.Initialized))`
   - If `App` is null, we proceed to add timeout (good).
   - If `App` is not null and `App.Initialized` is `false`, `!App.Initialized` is `true`, so we return without adding the timeout. This is the bug!

The problem is: when `AutoSpin` is set to `true` before `App.Init()` is called (which is typical - you set properties then call `app.Init()`), the timeout is not added because `App.Initialized` is false. And there's no mechanism to add the timeout later when the app becomes initialized.

Let me check if there's an `InitializedChanged` event handler that could trigger `AddAutoSpinTimeout`.

Looking at the code, there's no subscription to `App.InitializedChanged` or `View.Initialized`. So the timeout is never added if `AutoSpin` is set before `App.Init()`.

Actually wait, let me re-read the condition more carefully:

```csharp
if (App is { } && (_timeout is { } || !App.Initialized))
{
    return;
}
```

This says: return (don't add timeout) if:
- App exists AND (_timeout exists OR App is NOT initialized)

So the timeout is only added when:
- App is null, OR
- App exists AND _timeout is null AND App IS initialized

The intent seems to be: "Only add the timeout if the app is initialized." But the problem is that if you set `AutoSpin = true` before the app is initialized, the timeout is never added, and nothing re-attempts to add it later.

The fix should be to subscribe to `App.InitializedChanged` and add the timeout when the app becomes initialized. Or we could simplify the logic.

Let me also check the `IDesignable.EnableForDesign()` method at line 306:
```csharp
bool IDesignable.EnableForDesign ()
{
    Style = new SpinnerStyle.Points ();
    SpinReverse = true;
    AutoSpin = true;
    return true;
}
```

This also sets `AutoSpin = true` - presumably during design time when the app might not be initialized.

Let me look at how other views handle this pattern:

   136	                                       }

   152	                                       }

   155	                                   }
   156	                                   else

   173	
   174	        void SetCustom ()

   176	            if (customField.Text.Length > 0)

   188	                }

   193	                {
   194	                    str.Add (c.ToString ());
   195	                }
   196

   198	            }
   199	            else
   200	            {
   201	                spinner.Visible = false;
   202	            }
   203	        }
   204

So `App` traverses up the view hierarchy. When `AutoSpin = true` is set, the spinner may not yet be added to a view hierarchy that has `App` set. But in the PR description example, `main.Add(spinner)` happens before `app.Run(main)`, and `App` is set during `Run`.

Wait, actually let me re-check. The PR description shows:
```csharp
using IApplication app = Application.Create ();
app.Init ();
using Window main = new () { ... };
SpinnerView spinner = new () { AutoSpin = true };
main.Add (spinner);
app.Run (main);
```

In this case, when `AutoSpin = true` is set, `spinner` is not yet added to `main`, and `main` is not yet added to `app`. So `spinner.App` would be null (since its `_app` is null and it has no `SuperView`). 

When `App` is null, the condition:
```csharp
if (App is { } && (_timeout is { } || !App.Initialized))
```
evaluates to `false` (because `App is { }` is false), so we proceed to:
```csharp
_timeout = App?.AddTimeout(...)
```
But `App` is null, so `App?.AddTimeout(...)` returns null, and `_timeout` is set to null! So the timeout is never actually added.

Then later when `app.Run(main)` is called, the spinner gets its `App` property set (through the view hierarchy), but `_timeout` is null and nothing re-triggers `AddAutoSpinTimeout`.

So the fundamental issue is that `AddAutoSpinTimeout` doesn't actually add a timeout when `App` is null. And there's no mechanism to retry when `App` becomes available.

Now, let me also check if there's a similar issue with the condition `!App.Initialized`. Even if `App` is set, if it's not yet initialized, the timeout won't be added.

Let me think about the proper fix:

1. We should try to add the timeout when `AutoSpin` is set to true.
2. If `App` is null or not initialized, we should defer adding the timeout until `App` becomes available and initialized.
3. We could subscribe to `Initialized` event on the view or `App.InitializedChanged` to add the timeout later.

   100	    public SessionToken? Begin (IRunnable runnable)
   101	    {
   102	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull (runnable);
   103	
   104	        if (runnable.IsRunning)
   105	        {
   106	            throw new ArgumentException (@"The runnable is already running.", nameof (runnable));
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        // Create session token
   110	        SessionToken token = new (runnable);
   111	
   112	        Trace.Lifecycle (MainThreadId.ToString (), "Begin", "(token.Runnable as Runnable)?.ToIdentifyingString ()");
   113	
   114	        // Get old IsRunning value BEFORE any stack changes (safe - cached value)
   115	        bool oldIsRunning = runnable.IsRunning;
   116	
   117	        // Raise IsRunningChanging OUTSIDE lock (false -> true) - can be canceled
   118	        if (runnable.RaiseIsRunningChanging (oldIsRunning, true))
   119	        {
   120	            // Starting was canceled
   121	            return null;
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        // Set the application reference in the runnable
   125	        runnable.SetApp (this);
   126	
   127	        // Ensure the mouse is ungrabbed
   128	        Mouse.UngrabMouse ();
   129	
   130	        Navigation?.SetFocused (null);
   131	
   132	        IRunnable? previousTop = null;
   133	
   134	        // CRITICAL SECTION - Atomic stack + cached state update
   135	        lock (_sessionStackLock)
   136	        {
   137	            // Get the previous top BEFORE pushing new token
   138	            if (SessionStack?.TryPeek (out SessionToken? previousToken) == true && previousToken.Runnable is { })
   139	            {
   140	                previousTop = previousToken.Runnable;
   141	            }
   142	
   143	            if (previousTop == runnable)
   144	            {
   145	                throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException (nameof (runnable), runnable, @"Attempt to Run the runnable that's already the top runnable.");
   146	            }
   147	
   148	            // Push token onto SessionStack
   149	            SessionStack?.Push (token);
   150	
   151	            TopRunnable = runnable;
   152	
   153	            // Update cached state atomically - IsRunning and IsModal are now consistent
   154	            SessionBegun?.Invoke (this, new SessionTokenEventArgs (token));
   155	            runnable.SetIsRunning (true);
   156	            runnable.SetIsModal (true);
   157	
   158	            // Previous top is no longer modal
   159	            previousTop?.SetIsModal (false);
   160	        }
   161	
   162	        // END CRITICAL SECTION - IsRunning/IsModal now thread-safe
   163	
   164	        // Fire events AFTER lock released (avoid deadlocks in event handlers)
   165	        previousTop?.RaiseIsModalChangedEvent (false);
   166	
   167	        runnable.RaiseIsRunningChangedEvent (true);
   168	        runnable.RaiseIsModalChangedEvent (true);
   169	
   170	        LayoutAndDraw ();
   171	
   172	        return token;
   173	    }
   174	
   175	    #endregion Session Lifecycle - Begin
   176	
   177	    #region Session Lifecycle - Run
   178	
   179	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   180	    [RequiresUnreferencedCode ("AOT")]
   181	    [RequiresDynamicCode ("AOT")]
   182	    public IApplication Run<TRunnable> (Func<Exception, bool>? errorHandler = null, string? driverName = null) where TRunnable : IRunnable, new ()
   183	    {
   184	        if (!Initialized)
   185	        {
   186	            // Init() has NOT been called. Auto-initialize as per interface contract.
   187	            Init (driverName);
   188	        }
   189	
   190	        if (Driver is null)
   191	        {
   192	            throw new InvalidOperationException (@"Driver is null after Init.");
   193	        }
   194	
   195	        TRunnable runnable = new ();
   196	        Run (runnable, errorHandler);
   197	
   198	        // We created the runnable, so dispose it if it's disposable
   199	        if (runnable is IDisposable disposable)
   200	        {
   201	            disposable.Dispose ();
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        return this;
   205	    }
   206	
   207	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   208	    public object? Run (IRunnable runnable, Func<Exception, bool>? errorHandler = null)
   209	    {
   210	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull (runnable);
   211	
   212	        if (!Initialized)
   213	        {
   214	            throw new NotInitializedException (@"Init must be called before Run.");
   215	        }
   216	
   217	        // Begin the session (adds to stack, raises IsRunningChanging/IsRunningChanged)
   218	        SessionToken? token;
   219	
   220	        // Find it on the stack
   221	        token = runnable.IsRunning ? SessionStack?.FirstOrDefault (st => st.Runnable == runnable) : Begin (runnable);
   222	
   223	        if (token is null)
   224	        {
   225	            Logging.Warning (@"Run - Begin session failed or was cancelled.");
   226	
   227	            return null;
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        try
   231	        {
   232	            // All runnables block until RequestStop() is called
   233	            RunLoop (runnable, errorHandler);
   234	        }
   235	        finally
   236	        {
   237	            // End the session (raises IsRunningChanging/IsRunningChanged, pops from stack)
   238	            End (token);
   239	        }
   240	
   241	        return token.Result;
   242	    }
   243	
   244	    private void RunLoop (IRunnable runnable, Func<Exception, bool>? errorHandler)
   245	    {
   246	        runnable.StopRequested = false;
   247	
   248	        // Main loop - blocks until RequestStop() is called
   249	        // Note: IsRunning is now a cached property, safe to check each iteration
   250	        var firstIteration = true;
   251	
   252	        Trace.Lifecycle (MainThreadId.ToString (), "Run", $"{(runnable as Runnable)?.ToIdentifyingString ()}");
   253	
   254	        while (runnable is { StopRequested: false, IsRunning: true })
   255	        {
   256	            if (Coordinator is null)
   257	            {
   258	                throw new Exception ($"{nameof (IMainLoopCoordinator)} inexplicably became null during Run");
   259	            }
   260	
   261	            try
   262	            {
   263	                // Process one iteration of the event loop
   264	                Coordinator.RunIteration ();
   265	            }
   266	            catch (Exception ex)
   267	            {
   268	                if (errorHandler is null || !errorHandler (ex))
   269	                {
   270	                    throw;
   271	                }
   272	            }
   273	
   274	            if (StopAfterFirstIteration && firstIteration)
   275	            {
   276	                Trace.Lifecycle (MainThreadId.ToString (),
   277	                                 "Run",
   278	                                 $"{(runnable as Runnable)?.ToIdentifyingString ()} Stopping after first iteration as requested");
   279	                RequestStop (runnable);
   280	            }
   281	
   282	            firstIteration = false;
   283	        }
   284	
   285	        Trace.Lifecycle (MainThreadId.ToString (), "Run", $"{(runnable as Runnable)?.ToIdentifyingString ()} Stopped");
   286	    }
   287	
   288	    #endregion Session Lifecycle - Run
   289	
   290	    #region Session Lifecycle - End
   291	
   292	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   293	    public void End (SessionToken token)
   294	    {
   295	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull (token);
   296	
   297	        if (token.Runnable is null)
   298	        {
   299	            return; // Already ended
   300	        }
   301	
   302	        Trace.Lifecycle (MainThreadId.ToString (), "End", $"{(token.Runnable as Runnable)?.ToIdentifyingString ()}");
   303	
   304	        if (Popovers?.GetActivePopover () is { Visible: true } visiblePopover)
   305	        {
   306	            ApplicationPopover.HideWithQuitCommand (visiblePopover);
   307	        }
   308	
   309	        IRunnable runnable = token.Runnable;
   310	
   311	        // Get old IsRunning value (safe - cached value)
   312	        bool oldIsRunning = runnable.IsRunning;
   313	
   314	        // Raise IsRunningChanging OUTSIDE lock (true -> false) - can be canceled
   315	        // This is where Result should be extracted!
   316	        if (runnable.RaiseIsRunningChanging (oldIsRunning, false))
   317	        {
   318	            // Stopping was canceled - do not proceed with End
   319	            return;
   320	        }
   321	
   322	        bool wasModal = runnable.IsModal;
   323	        IRunnable? previousRunnable = null;
   324	
   325	        // CRITICAL SECTION - Atomic stack + cached state update
   326	        lock (_sessionStackLock)
   327	        {
   328	            // Pop token from SessionStack
   329	            if (wasModal && SessionStack?.TryPop (out SessionToken? popped) == true && popped == token)
   330	            {
   331	                // Restore previous top runnable
   332	                if (SessionStack?.TryPeek (out SessionToken? previousToken) == true && previousToken.Runnable is { })
   333	                {
   334	                    previousRunnable = previousToken.Runnable;
   335	
   336	                    // Previous runnable becomes modal again
   337	                    previousRunnable.SetIsModal (true);
   338	                }
   339	            }
   340	
   341	            // Update cached state atomically - IsRunning and IsModal are now consistent
   342	            runnable.SetIsRunning (false);
   343	            runnable.SetIsModal (false);
   344	        }
   345	
   346	        // END CRITICAL SECTION - IsRunning/IsModal now thread-safe
   347	
   348	        // Fire events AFTER lock released
   349	        if (wasModal)
   350	        {
   351	            runnable.RaiseIsModalChangedEvent (false);
   352	        }
   353	
   354	        TopRunnable = null;
   355	
   356	        if (previousRunnable != null)
   357	        {
   358	            TopRunnable = previousRunnable;
   359	            previousRunnable.RaiseIsModalChangedEvent (true);
   360	        }
   361	
   362	        Mouse.UngrabMouse ();
   363	
   364	        runnable.RaiseIsRunningChangedEvent (false);
   365	
   366	        token.Result = runnable.Result;
   367	
   368	        _result = token.Result;
   369	
   370	        Trace.Lifecycle (MainThreadId.ToString (), "End", $"{(token.Runnable as Runnable)?.ToIdentifyingString ()} - Result: {_result ?? Glyphs.Null}");
   371	
   372	        // Clear the Runnable from the token
   373	        token.Runnable = null;
   374	        SessionEnded?.Invoke (this, new SessionTokenEventArgs (token));
   375	    }
   376	
   377	    #endregion Session Lifecycle - End
   378	
   379	    #region Session Lifecycle - RequestStop
   380	
   381	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   382	    public void RequestStop () => RequestStop (null);
   383	
   384	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   385	    public void RequestStop (IRunnable? runnable)
   386	    {
   387	        // Get the runnable to stop
   388	        if (runnable is null)
   389	        {
   390	            // Try to get from TopRunnable
   391	            if (TopRunnableView is IRunnable r)
   392	            {
   393	                runnable = r;
   394	            }
   395	            else
   396	            {
   397	                return;
   398	            }
   399	        }
   400	
   401	        Trace.Lifecycle (MainThreadId.ToString (), "Run", $"{(runnable as Runnable)?.ToIdentifyingString ()}");
   402	
   403	        runnable.StopRequested = true;
   404	
   405	        // Note: The End() method will be called from the finally block in Run()
   406	        // and that's where IsRunningChanging/IsRunningChanged will be raised
   407	    }
   408	
   409	    #endregion Session Lifecycle - RequestStop
   410	}

Now I see the key line: at line 125, `runnable.SetApp(this)` is called during `Begin()`. This sets the `App` property on the runnable (the top-level view). Then through the `GetApp()` traversal, all child views can find the App.

So the fix should be: when `AutoSpin` is set to `true`, if we can't add the timeout immediately (because `App` is null or not initialized), we should defer it until the view is initialized and has access to `App`.

The best approach would be to override `EndInit` or subscribe to the `Initialized` event, and add the timeout there if `AutoSpin` is true.

But wait, let me also check if there's a simpler approach. Let me look at the condition again:

```csharp
if (App is { } && (_timeout is { } || !App.Initialized))
{
    return;
}
```

What if we just remove the `!App.Initialized` check? Let me think about this...

If we remove `!App.Initialized`:
- When `App` is null: we proceed to `App?.AddTimeout(...)` which returns null (timeout not added). But `AutoSpin` will return `false` because `_timeout` is null! 
- When `App` is not null but not initialized: we would try to add a timeout. But `TimedEvents` might not be initialized yet.

   221	    ///     View implements <see cref="ISupportInitializeNotification"/> to allow for more sophisticated initialization.
   222	    /// </summary>
   223	    public event EventHandler? Initialized;
   224	
   225	    /// <summary>
   226	    ///     Get or sets if  the <see cref="View"/> has been initialized (via <see cref="ISupportInitialize.BeginInit"/>
   227	    ///     and <see cref="ISupportInitialize.EndInit"/>).
   228	    /// </summary>
   229	    /// <para>
   230	    ///     If first-run-only initialization is preferred, overrides to
   231	    ///     <see cref="ISupportInitializeNotification.IsInitialized"/> can be implemented, in which case the
   232	    ///     <see cref="ISupportInitialize"/> methods will only be called if
   233	    ///     <see cref="ISupportInitializeNotification.IsInitialized"/> is <see langword="false"/>. This allows proper
   234	    ///     <see cref="View"/> inheritance hierarchies to override base class layout code optimally by doing so only on first
   235	    ///     run, instead of on every run.
   236	    /// </para>
   237	    public virtual bool IsInitialized { get; set; }
   238	
   239	    /// <summary>Signals the View that initialization is starting. See <see cref="ISupportInitialize"/>.</summary>
   240	    /// <remarks>
   241	    ///     <para>
   242	    ///         Views can opt-in to more sophisticated initialization by implementing overrides to
   243	    ///         <see cref="ISupportInitialize.BeginInit"/> and <see cref="ISupportInitialize.EndInit"/> which will be called
   244	    ///         when the <see cref="SuperView"/> is initialized.
   245	    ///     </para>
   246	    ///     <para>
   247	    ///         If first-run-only initialization is preferred, overrides to <see cref="ISupportInitializeNotification"/> can
   248	    ///         be implemented too, in which case the <see cref="ISupportInitialize"/> methods will only be called if
   249	    ///         <see cref="ISupportInitializeNotification.IsInitialized"/> is <see langword="false"/>. This allows proper
   250	    ///         <see cref="View"/> inheritance hierarchies to override base class layout code optimally by doing so only on
   251	    ///         first run, instead of on every run.
   252	    ///     </para>
   253	    /// </remarks>
   254	    public virtual void BeginInit ()
   255	    {
   256	        if (IsInitialized)
   257	        {
   258	            throw new InvalidOperationException ("The view is already initialized.");
   259	        }
   260	#if AUTO_CANFOCUS
   261	        _oldCanFocus = CanFocus;
   262	        _oldTabIndex = _tabIndex;
   263	#endif
   264	
   265	        BeginInitAdornments ();
   266	
   267	        if (InternalSubViews.Count <= 0)
   268	        {
   269	            return;
   270	        }
   271	
   272	        foreach (View view in InternalSubViews)
   273	        {
   274	            if (!view.IsInitialized)
   275	            {
   276	                view.BeginInit ();
   277	            }
   278	        }
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    // TODO: Implement logic that allows EndInit to throw if BeginInit has not been called
   282	    // TODO: See EndInit_Called_Without_BeginInit_Throws test.
   283	
   284	    /// <summary>Signals the View that initialization is ending. See <see cref="ISupportInitialize"/>.</summary>
   285	    /// <remarks>
   286	    ///     <para>Initializes all SubViews and Invokes the <see cref="Initialized"/> event.</para>
   287	    /// </remarks>
   288	    public virtual void EndInit ()
   289	    {
   290	        if (IsInitialized)
   291	        {
   292	            throw new InvalidOperationException ("The view is already initialized.");
   293	        }
   294	
   295	        IsInitialized = true;
   296	
   297	        EndInitAdornments ();
   298	
   299	        // TODO: Move these into ViewText.cs as EndInit_Text() to consolidate.
   300	        // TODO: Verify UpdateTextDirection really needs to be called here.
   301	        // These calls were moved from BeginInit as they access Viewport which is indeterminate until EndInit is called.
   302	        UpdateTextDirection (TextDirection);
   303	        UpdateTextFormatterText ();
   304	
   305	        foreach (View view in InternalSubViews)
   306	        {
   307	            if (!view.IsInitialized)
   308	            {
   309	                view.EndInit ();
   310	            }
   311	        }
   312	
   313	        // Force a layout each time a View is initialized
   314	        Layout ();
   315	
   316	        // Complex layout scenarios (e.g. DimAuto and PosAlign) may require multiple layouts to be performed.
   317	        // Thus, we call SetNeedsLayout() to ensure that the layout is performed at least once.
   318	        SetNeedsLayout ();
   319	
   320	        Initialized?.Invoke (this, EventArgs.Empty);
   321	    }
   322	
   323	    #endregion Constructors and Initialization
   324	
   325	    #region Visibility
   326

   328	    public bool Enabled
   329	    {
   330	        get;
   331	        set
   332	        {
   333	            if (field == value)
   334	            {
   335	                return;
   336	            }
   337	
   338	            field = value;
   339	
   340	            if (!field && HasFocus)

The fix I propose:
1. Change `AddAutoSpinTimeout` to handle the case when `App` is null or not initialized by subscribing to the `Initialized` event (or `App.InitializedChanged`).
2. When the initialization happens, try to add the timeout again.

    11	/// <summary>Displays a spinning glyph or combinations of glyphs to indicate progress or activity</summary>
    12	/// <remarks>
    13	///     By default, animation only occurs when you call <see cref="SpinnerView.AdvanceAnimation(bool)"/>. Use
    14	///     <see cref="AutoSpin"/> to make the automate calls to <see cref="SpinnerView.AdvanceAnimation(bool)"/>.
    15	/// </remarks>
    16	public class SpinnerView : View, IDesignable
    17	{
    18	    private const int DEFAULT_DELAY = 130;
    19	    private static readonly SpinnerStyle DEFAULT_STYLE = new SpinnerStyle.Line ();
    20

    22	    private bool _bounceReverse;
    23	    private int _currentIdx;

    48	    {
    49	        get => _timeout != null;
    50	        set
    51	        {
    52	            if (value)
    53	            {
    54	                AddAutoSpinTimeout ();
    55	            }
    56	            else
    57	            {
    58	                RemoveAutoSpinTimeout ();
    59	            }
    60	        }

   112	
   113	    /// <summary>
   114	    ///     Advances the animation frame and notifies main loop that repainting needs to happen. Repeated calls are
   115	    ///     ignored based on <see cref="SpinDelay"/>.
   116	    /// </summary>
   117	    /// <remarks>Ensure this method is called on the main UI thread e.g. via <see cref="IApplication.Invoke(Action)"/></remarks>
   118	    public void AdvanceAnimation (bool setNeedsDraw = true)
   119	    {
   120	        if (DateTime.Now - _lastRender > TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds (SpinDelay))
   121	        {
   122	            if (Sequence is { Length: > 1 })
   123	            {
   124	                var d = 1;
   125	
   126	                if ((_bounceReverse && !SpinReverse) || (!_bounceReverse && SpinReverse))
   127	                {
   128	                    d = -1;
   129	                }
   130	
   131	                _currentIdx += d;
   132	
   133	                if (_currentIdx >= Sequence.Length)
   134	                {
   135	                    if (SpinBounce)
   136	                    {
   137	                        _bounceReverse = !SpinReverse;
   138	
   139	                        _currentIdx = Sequence.Length - 1;
   140	                    }
   141	                    else
   142	                    {
   143	                        _currentIdx = 0;
   144	                    }
   145	                }
   146	
   147	                if (_currentIdx < 0)
   148	                {
   149	                    if (SpinBounce)
   150	                    {
   151	                        _bounceReverse = SpinReverse;
   152	
   153	                        _currentIdx = 1;
   154	                    }
   155	                    else
   156	                    {
   157	                        _currentIdx = Sequence.Length - 1;
   158	                    }
   159	                }
   160	            }
   161	
   162	            _lastRender = DateTime.Now;
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        if (setNeedsDraw)
   166	        {
   167	            SetNeedsDraw ();
   168	        }
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   172	    protected override bool OnClearingViewport () { return true; }
   173	
   174	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   175	    protected override bool OnDrawingContent (DrawContext? context)
   176	    {
   177	        Render ();
   178	
   179	        return true;
   180	    }
   181	
   182	    /// <summary>
   183	    ///     Renders the current frame of the spinner.
   184	    /// </summary>
   185	    public void Render ()
   186	    {
   187	        if (Sequence is { Length: > 0 } && _currentIdx < Sequence.Length)
   188	        {
   189	            Move (Viewport.X, Viewport.Y);
   190	            AddStr (Sequence [_currentIdx]);
   191	        }
   192	    }
   193	
   194	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   195	    protected override void Dispose (bool disposing)
   196	    {
   197	        RemoveAutoSpinTimeout ();
   198	
   199	        base.Dispose (disposing);
   200	    }
   201	
   202	    private void AddAutoSpinTimeout ()
   203	    {
   204	        // Only add timeout if we are initialized and not already spinning
   205	        if (App is { } && (_timeout is { } || !App.Initialized))
   206	        {
   207	            return;
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        _timeout = App?.AddTimeout (
   211	                                           TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds (SpinDelay),
   212	                                           () =>
   213	                                           {
   214	                                               App.Invoke ((_) => AdvanceAnimation ());
   215	
   216	                                               return true;
   217	                                           }
   218	                                          );
   219	    }
   220	
   221	    private bool GetIsAsciiOnly ()
   222	    {
   223	        if (HasSpecialCharacters)
   224	        {
   225	            return false;
   226	        }
   227	
   228	        if (_sequence is { Length: > 0 })
   229	        {
   230	            foreach (string frame in _sequence)
   231	            {
   232	                foreach (char c in frame)
   233	                {
   234	                    if (!char.IsAscii (c))
   235	                    {
   236	                        return false;
   237	                    }
   238	                }
   239	            }
   240	
   241	            return true;
   242	        }
   243	
   244	        return true;
   245	    }
   246	
   247	    private int GetSpinnerWidth ()
   248	    {
   249	        var max = 0;
   250	
   251	        if (_sequence is { Length: > 0 })
   252	        {
   253	            foreach (string frame in _sequence)
   254	            {
   255	                if (frame.Length > max)
   256	                {
   257	                    max = frame.Length;
   258	                }
   259	            }
   260	        }
   261	
   262	        return max;
   263	    }
   264	
   265	    private void RemoveAutoSpinTimeout ()
   266	    {
   267	        if (_timeout is { })
   268	        {
   269	            App?.RemoveTimeout (_timeout);
   270	            _timeout = null;
   271	        }
   272	    }
   273	
   274	    private void SetBounce (bool bounce) { _bounce = bounce; }
   275	
   276	    private void SetDelay (int delay)
   277	    {
   278	        if (delay > -1)
   279	        {
   280	            _delay = delay;
   281	        }
   282	    }
   283	
   284	    private void SetSequence (string [] frames)
   285	    {
   286	        if (frames is { Length: > 0 })
   287	        {
   288	            _style = new SpinnerStyle.Custom ();
   289	            _sequence = frames;
   290	            Width = GetSpinnerWidth ();
   291	        }
   292	    }
   293	
   294	    private void SetStyle (SpinnerStyle? style)
   295	    {
   296	        if (style is { })
   297	        {
   298	            _style = style;
   299	            _sequence = style.Sequence;
   300	            _delay = style.SpinDelay;
   301	            _bounce = style.SpinBounce;
   302	            Width = GetSpinnerWidth ();
   303	        }
   304	    }
   305	
   306	    bool IDesignable.EnableForDesign ()
   307	    {
   308	        Style = new SpinnerStyle.Points ();
   309	        SpinReverse = true;
   310	        AutoSpin = true;
   311	
   312	        return true;
   313	    }
   314	}

Now I understand the full picture. Let me implement the fix. The issue is:

1. In `AddAutoSpinTimeout`, when `App` is null, `App?.AddTimeout(...)` returns null.
2. When `App` is not null but not initialized, the method returns early.
3. There's no mechanism to retry when `App` becomes available/initialized.

The fix should:
1. Use the `Initialized` event to defer adding the timeout until the view (and its hierarchy) is initialized.
2. Also handle the case where `App` might become available after initialization (e.g., when added to a running application).

//------------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Windows Terminal supports Unicode and Emoji characters, but by default
// conhost shells (e.g., PowerShell and cmd.exe) do not. See
// <https://spectreconsole.net/best-practices>.
//------------------------------------------------------------------------------

namespace Terminal.Gui.Views;

/// <summary>Displays a spinning glyph or combinations of glyphs to indicate progress or activity</summary>
/// <remarks>
///     By default, animation only occurs when you call <see cref="SpinnerView.AdvanceAnimation(bool)"/>. Use
///     <see cref="AutoSpin"/> to make the automate calls to <see cref="SpinnerView.AdvanceAnimation(bool)"/>.
/// </remarks>
public class SpinnerView : View, IDesignable
{
    private const int DEFAULT_DELAY = 130;
    private static readonly SpinnerStyle DEFAULT_STYLE = new SpinnerStyle.Line ();

    private bool _autoSpin;
    private bool _bounce = DEFAULT_STYLE.SpinBounce;
    private bool _bounceReverse;
    private int _currentIdx;
    private int _delay = DEFAULT_STYLE.SpinDelay;
    private DateTime _lastRender = DateTime.MinValue;
    private string [] _sequence = DEFAULT_STYLE.Sequence;
    private SpinnerStyle _style = DEFAULT_STYLE;
    private object? _timeout;

    /// <summary>Creates a new instance of the <see cref="SpinnerView"/> class.</summary>
    public SpinnerView ()
    {
        Width = Dim.Auto (minimumContentDim: 1);
        Height = Dim.Auto (minimumContentDim: 1);
        _delay = DEFAULT_DELAY;
        _bounce = false;
        SpinReverse = false;
        SetStyle (DEFAULT_STYLE);

        Initialized += SpinnerView_Initialized;

        AdvanceAnimation ();
    }

    private void SpinnerView_Initialized (object? sender, EventArgs e)
    {
        if (_autoSpin)
        {
            AddAutoSpinTimeout ();
        }
    }

    /// <summary>
    ///     Gets or sets whether spinning should occur automatically or be manually triggered (e.g. from a background
    ///     task).
    /// </summary>
    public bool AutoSpin
    {
        get => _timeout != null;
        set
        {
            _autoSpin = value;
            if (value)
            {
                AddAutoSpinTimeout ();
            }
            else
            {
                RemoveAutoSpinTimeout ();
            }
        }
    }

    /// <summary>
    ///     Gets whether the current spinner style contains emoji or other special characters. Does not check Custom
    ///     sequences.
    /// </summary>
    public bool HasSpecialCharacters => _style.HasSpecialCharacters;

    /// <summary>Gets whether the current spinner style contains only ASCII characters.  Also checks Custom sequences.</summary>
    public bool IsAsciiOnly => GetIsAsciiOnly ();

    /// <summary>Gets or sets the animation frames used to animate the spinner.</summary>
    public string [] Sequence
    {
        get => _sequence;
        set => SetSequence (value);
    }

    /// <summary>
    ///     Gets or sets whether spinner should go back and forth through the frames rather than going to the end and
    ///     starting again at the beginning.
    /// </summary>
    public bool SpinBounce
    {
        get => _bounce;
        set => SetBounce (value);
    }

    /// <summary>Gets or sets the number of milliseconds to wait between characters in the animation.</summary>
    /// <remarks>
    ///     This is the maximum speed the spinner will rotate at.  You still need to call
    ///     <see cref="SpinnerView.AdvanceAnimation(bool)"/> or <see cref="SpinnerView.AutoSpin"/> to advance/start animation.
    /// </remarks>
    public int SpinDelay
    {
        get => _delay;
        set => SetDelay (value);
    }

    /// <summary>
    ///     Gets or sets whether spinner should go through the frames in reverse order. If SpinBounce is true, this sets
    ///     the starting order.
    /// </summary>
    public bool SpinReverse { get; set; }

    /// <summary>Gets or sets the Style used to animate the spinner.</summary>
    public SpinnerStyle Style
    {
        get => _style;
        set => SetStyle (value);
    }

    /// <summary>
    ///     Advances the animation frame and notifies main loop that repainting needs to happen. Repeated calls are
    ///     ignored based on <see cref="SpinDelay"/>.
    /// </summary>
    /// <remarks>Ensure this method is called on the main UI thread e.g. via <see cref="IApplication.Invoke(Action)"/></remarks>
    public void AdvanceAnimation (bool setNeedsDraw = true)
    {
        if (DateTime.Now - _lastRender > TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds (SpinDelay))
        {
            if (Sequence is { Length: > 1 })
            {
                var d = 1;

                if ((_bounceReverse && !SpinReverse) || (!_bounceReverse && SpinReverse))
                {
                    d = -1;
                }

                _currentIdx += d;

                if (_currentIdx >= Sequence.Length)
                {
                    if (SpinBounce)
                    {
                        _bounceReverse = !SpinReverse;

                        _currentIdx = Sequence.Length - 1;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        _currentIdx = 0;
                    }
                }

                if (_currentIdx < 0)
                {
                    if (SpinBounce)
                    {
                        _bounceReverse = SpinReverse;

                        _currentIdx = 1;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        _currentIdx = Sequence.Length - 1;
                    }
                }
            }

            _lastRender = DateTime.Now;
        }

        if (setNeedsDraw)
        {
            SetNeedsDraw ();
        }
    }

    /// <inheritdoc/>
    protected override bool OnClearingViewport () { return true; }

    /// <inheritdoc/>
    protected override bool OnDrawingContent (DrawContext? context)
    {
        Render ();

        return true;
    }

    /// <summary>
    ///     Renders the current frame of the spinner.
    /// </summary>
    public void Render ()
    {
        if (Sequence is { Length: > 0 } && _currentIdx < Sequence.Length)
        {
            Move (Viewport.X, Viewport.Y);
            AddStr (Sequence [_currentIdx]);
        }
    }

    /// <inheritdoc/>
    protected override void Dispose (bool disposing)
    {
        RemoveAutoSpinTimeout ();

        base.Dispose (disposing);
    }

    private void AddAutoSpinTimeout ()
    {
        // Only add timeout if we have an initialized app and are not already spinning
        if (App is null || _timeout is { })
        {
            return;
        }

        _timeout = App.AddTimeout (
                                   TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds (SpinDelay),
                                   () =>
                                   {
                                       App.Invoke ((_) => AdvanceAnimation ());

                                       return true;
                                   }
                                  );
    }

    private bool GetIsAsciiOnly ()
    {
        if (HasSpecialCharacters)
        {
            return false;
        }

        if (_sequence is { Length: > 0 })
        {
            foreach (string frame in _sequence)
            {
                foreach (char c in frame)
                {
                    if (!char.IsAscii (c))
                    {
                        return false;
                    }
                }
            }

            return true;
        }

        return true;
    }

    private int GetSpinnerWidth ()
    {
        var max = 0;

        if (_sequence is { Length: > 0 })
        {
            foreach (string frame in _sequence)
            {
                if (frame.Length > max)
                {
                    max = frame.Length;
                }
            }
        }

        return max;
    }

    private void RemoveAutoSpinTimeout ()
    {
        if (_timeout is { })
        {
            App?.RemoveTimeout (_timeout);
            _timeout = null;
        }
    }

    private void SetBounce (bool bounce) { _bounce = bounce; }

    private void SetDelay (int delay)
    {
        if (delay > -1)
        {
            _delay = delay;
        }
    }

    private void SetSequence (string [] frames)
    {
        if (frames is { Length: > 0 })
        {
            _style = new SpinnerStyle.Custom ();
            _sequence = frames;
            Width = GetSpinnerWidth ();
        }
    }

    private void SetStyle (SpinnerStyle? style)
    {
        if (style is { })
        {
            _style = style;
            _sequence = style.Sequence;
            _delay = style.SpinDelay;
            _bounce = style.SpinBounce;
            Width = GetSpinnerWidth ();
        }
    }

    bool IDesignable.EnableForDesign ()
    {
        Style = new SpinnerStyle.Points ();
        SpinReverse = true;
        AutoSpin = true;

        return true;
    }
}

    43	    ///     as SubViews from the Margin, Border, and Padding adornments.
    44	    /// </returns>
    45	    /// <remarks>
    46	    ///     <para>
    47	    ///         This method returns a snapshot of the SubViews at the time of the call. The collection is
    48	    ///         safe to iterate even if SubViews are added or removed during iteration.
    49	    ///     </para>
    50	    ///     <para>
    51	    ///         The order of SubViews in the returned collection is:

    57	    ///         </list>
    58	    ///     </para>
    59	    /// </remarks>
    60	    public virtual IReadOnlyCollection<View> GetSubViews (bool includeMargin = false, bool includeBorder = false, bool includePadding = false)
    61	    {
    62	        List<View> result = [];
    63	
    64	        // Add direct SubViews
    65	        result.AddRange (InternalSubViews);
    66	
    67	        if (includeMargin && Margin.View is { SubViews.Count: > 0 } && Margin.Thickness != Thickness.Empty)
    68	        {
    69	            // Add Margin SubViews
    70	            result.AddRange (Margin.View.SubViews);
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        if (includeBorder && Border.View is { SubViews.Count: > 0 } && Border.Thickness != Thickness.Empty)
    74	        {
    75	            // Add Border SubViews
    76	            result.AddRange (Border.View.SubViews);
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        if (includePadding && Padding.View is { SubViews.Count: > 0 } && Padding.Thickness != Thickness.Empty)
    80	        {
    81	            // Add Padding SubViews
    82	            result.AddRange (Padding.View.SubViews);
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        return result.AsReadOnly ();
    86	    }

   155	    /// <summary>
   156	    ///     Adds a SubView (child) to this view at the specified index in the <see cref="SubViews"/> list.
   157	    /// </summary>
   158	    /// <remarks>

   160	    ///         The Views that have been added to this view can be retrieved via the <see cref="SubViews"/> property.

   165	    ///     <para>
   166	    ///         SubViews will be disposed when this View is disposed. In other-words, calling this method causes
   167	    ///         the lifecycle of the subviews to be transferred to this View.
   168	    ///     </para>
   169	    ///     <para>
   170	    ///         Calls/Raises the <see cref="OnSubViewAdded"/>/<see cref="SubViewAdded"/> event.
   171	    ///     </para>
   172	    ///     <para>
   173	    ///         The <see cref="OnSuperViewChanged"/>/<see cref="SuperViewChanged"/> event will be raised on the added View.
   174	    ///     </para>
   175	    /// </remarks>
   176	    /// <param name="index">The index at which to insert the view.</param>
   177	    /// <param name="view">The view to add.</param>
   178	    /// <returns>The view that was added.</returns>
   179	    /// <seealso cref="Remove(View)"/>
   180	    /// <seealso cref="RemoveAll"/>
   181	    /// <seealso cref="OnSubViewAdded"/>
   182	    /// <seealso cref="SubViewAdded"/>
   183	    /// <seealso cref="OnSuperViewChanging"/>
   184	    /// <seealso cref="SuperViewChanging"/>
   185	    /// <seealso cref="OnSuperViewChanged"/>
   186	    /// <seealso cref="SuperViewChanged"/>
   187	    public View? AddAt (int index, View? view)
   188	    {
   189	        if (view is null)
   190	        {
   191	            return null;
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        ArgumentOutOfRangeException.ThrowIfNegative (index);
   195	        ArgumentOutOfRangeException.ThrowIfGreaterThan (index, InternalSubViews.Count);
   196	
   197	        //Debug.Assert (view.SuperView is null, $"{view} already has a SuperView: {view.SuperView}.");
   198	        if (view.SuperView is { })
   199	        {
   200	            Logging.Warning ($"{view} already has a SuperView: {view.SuperView}.");
   201	        }
   202	
   203	        //Debug.Assert (!InternalSubViews.Contains (view), $"{view} has already been Added to {this}.");
   204	        if (InternalSubViews.Contains (view))
   205	        {
   206	            Logging.Warning ($"{view} has already been Added to {this}.");
   207	        }
   208	
   209	        // TODO: Add AddingSubView event
   210	        if (this is MarginView)
   211	        {
   212	            if (view is not ShadowView)
   213	            {
   214	                throw new InvalidOperationException ("SubViews of Margin are not supported.");
   215	            }
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        // TODO: Make this thread safe
   219	        InternalSubViews.Insert (index, view);
   220	
   221	        // Try to set the SuperView - this may be cancelled
   222	        if (!view.SetSuperView (this))
   223	        {
   224	            InternalSubViews.RemoveAt (index);
   225	
   226	            // The change was cancelled
   227	            return null;
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        // Ensure views don't have focus when being added
   231	        view.HasFocus = false;
   232	
   233	        if (view is { Enabled: true, Visible: true, CanFocus: true })
   234	        {
   235	            // Add will cause the newly added subview to gain focus if it's focusable
   236	            if (HasFocus)
   237	            {
   238	                view.SetFocus ();
   239	            }
   240	        }
   241	
   242	        if (view.Enabled && !Enabled)
   243	        {
   244	            view.Enabled = false;
   245	        }
   246	
   247	        // Raise event indicating a subview has been added
   248	        // We do this before Init.
   249	        RaiseSubViewAdded (view);
   250	
   251	        if (IsInitialized && !view.IsInitialized)
   252	        {
   253	            view.BeginInit ();
   254	            view.EndInit ();
   255	        }
   256	
   257	        SetNeedsDraw ();
   258	        SetNeedsLayout ();
   259	
   260	        return view;
   261	    }

2026-05-29 12:45:27,104 - INFO - swea-agent-gui-cs__Terminal.Gui-4882 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I see the key information at lines 251-255:

```csharp
if (IsInitialized && !view.IsInitialized)
{
    view.BeginInit ();
    view.EndInit ();
}
```

So when a view is added to another view that is already initialized, `BeginInit()` and `EndInit()` are called on the added view, which fires the `Initialized` event. This means:

1. In the PR description scenario: `app.Init()` is called first, then `main.Add(spinner)` is called. But is `main` initialized at that point? `main` was just created with `new Window()`, so `main.IsInitialized` is `false`. Therefore, adding spinner to main does NOT trigger `EndInit` on spinner.

2. Later, `app.Run(main)` calls `Begin(main)`, which doesn't trigger initialization either.

So when does initialization happen? Let me check `Begin` again... Actually, let me look at where `BeginInit`/`EndInit` are called for the top-level window:

     2	
     3	/// <summary>
     4	///     Base implementation of <see cref="IRunnable"/> for views that can be run as blocking sessions without returning a
     5	///     result.
     6	/// </summary>
     7	/// <remarks>
     8	///     <para>
     9	///         Views that don't need to return a result can derive from this class instead of <see cref="Runnable{TResult}"/>.
    10	///     </para>
    11	///     <para>
    12	///         This class provides default implementations of the <see cref="IRunnable"/> interface
    13	///         following the Terminal.Gui Cancellable Work Pattern (CWP).
    14	///     </para>
    15	///     <para>
    16	///         For views that need to return a result, use <see cref="Runnable{TResult}"/> instead.
    17	///     </para>
    18	/// </remarks>
    19	public class Runnable : View, IRunnable
    20	{
    21	    // Cached state - eliminates race conditions from stack queries
    22	
    23	    /// <summary>
    24	    ///     Constructs a new instance of the <see cref="Runnable"/> class.
    25	    /// </summary>
    26	    public Runnable ()
    27	    {
    28	        CanFocus = true;
    29	        TabStop = TabBehavior.TabGroup;
    30	        Arrangement = ViewArrangement.Overlapped;
    31	        Width = Dim.Fill ();
    32	        Height = Dim.Fill ();
    33	        SchemeName = SchemeManager.SchemesToSchemeName (Schemes.Runnable);
    34	    }
    35	
    36	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    37	    public object? Result { get; set; }
    38	
    39	    #region IRunnable Implementation - IsRunning (from base interface)
    40	
    41	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    42	    public void SetApp (IApplication app) => App = app;
    43

    45	    public bool IsRunning { get; private set; }
    46	
    47	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    48	    public void SetIsRunning (bool value) => IsRunning = value;
    49	
    50	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    51	    public virtual void RequestStop () =>
    52	
    53	        // Use the IRunnable-specific RequestStop if the App supports it
    54	        App?.RequestStop (this);
    55	
    56	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    57	    public bool RaiseIsRunningChanging (bool oldIsRunning, bool newIsRunning)
    58	    {
    59	        // Clear previous result when starting (for non-generic Runnable)
    60	        // Derived Runnable<TResult> will clear its typed Result in OnIsRunningChanging override
    61	        if (newIsRunning)
    62	        {
    63	            Result = null;
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        // CWP Phase 1: Virtual method (pre-notification)
    67	        if (OnIsRunningChanging (oldIsRunning, newIsRunning))
    68	        {
    69	            return true; // Canceled
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        // CWP Phase 2: Event notification
    73	        bool newValue = newIsRunning;
    74	        CancelEventArgs<bool> args = new (in oldIsRunning, ref newValue);
    75	        IsRunningChanging?.Invoke (this, args);
    76	
    77	        return args.Cancel;
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    81	    public event EventHandler<CancelEventArgs<bool>>? IsRunningChanging;
    82	
    83	    /// <inheritdoc/>
    84	    public void RaiseIsRunningChangedEvent (bool newIsRunning)
    85	    {
    86	        // Initialize if needed when starting
    87	        if (newIsRunning && !IsInitialized)
    88	        {
    89	            BeginInit ();
    90	            EndInit ();
    91	
    92	            // Initialized event is raised by View.EndInit()
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        // CWP Phase 3: Post-notification (work already done by Application.Begin/End)
    96	        OnIsRunningChanged (newIsRunning);
    97	
    98	        EventArgs<bool> args = new (newIsRunning);
    99	        IsRunningChanged?.Invoke (this, args);
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    /// <inheritdoc/>
   103	    public event EventHandler<EventArgs<bool>>? IsRunningChanged;
   104	
   105	    /// <summary>
   106	    ///     Called before <see cref="IsRunningChanging"/> event. Override to cancel state change or perform cleanup.
   107	    /// </summary>
   108	    /// <param name="oldIsRunning">The current value of <see cref="IsRunning"/>.</param>
   109	    /// <param name="newIsRunning">The new value of <see cref="IsRunning"/> (true = starting, false = stopping).</param>
   110	    /// <returns><see langword="true"/> to cancel; <see langword="false"/> to proceed.</returns>
   111	    /// <remarks>
   112	    ///     <para>
   113	    ///         Default implementation returns <see langword="false"/> (allow change).
   114	    ///     </para>
   115	    ///     <para>
   116	    ///         <b>IMPORTANT</b>: When <paramref name="newIsRunning"/> is <see langword="false"/> (stopping), this is the ideal
   117	    ///         place to perform cleanup or validation before the runnable is removed from the stack.
   118	    ///     </para>
   119	    ///     <example>
   120	    ///         <code>
   121	    /// protected override bool OnIsRunningChanging (bool oldIsRunning, bool newIsRunning)
   122	    /// {
   123	    ///     if (!newIsRunning)  // Stopping
   124	    ///     {
   125	    ///         // Check if user wants to save first
   126	    ///         if (HasUnsavedChanges ())
   127	    ///         {
   128	    ///             int result = MessageBox.Query (App, "Save?", "Save changes?", Strings.btnNo, Strings.btnYes);
   129	    ///             if (result == 0) return true;  // Cancel stopping
   130	    ///             if (result == 1) Save ();
   131	    ///         }
   132	    ///     }
   133	    /// 
   134	    ///     return base.OnIsRunningChanging (oldIsRunning, newIsRunning);
   135	    /// }
   136	    /// </code>
   137	    ///     </example>
   138	    /// </remarks>
   139	    protected virtual bool OnIsRunningChanging (bool oldIsRunning, bool newIsRunning) => false;
   140

   143	    /// </summary>

   145	    /// <remarks>
   146	    ///     Default implementation does nothing. Overrides should call base to ensure extensibility.
   147	    /// </remarks>
   148	    protected virtual void OnIsRunningChanged (bool newIsRunning)
   149	    {
   150	        // Default: no-op
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    #endregion

   159

   162

   165

   168	    {
   169	        if (newIsModal)
